  // Efectos optimizados para el nuevo diseño limpio
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const serviceCards = document.querySelectorAll('.clean-service-card');
    
    serviceCards.forEach(function(card) {
      // Efecto de entrada suave y limpio
      card.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
        // Elevación sutil sin distorsión
        this.style.transform = 'translateY(-6px)';
        this.style.transition = 'all 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)';
        
        // Sombra más pronunciada pero elegante
        this.style.boxShadow = '0 25px 50px -12px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15)';
        
        // Animación sutil del icono
        const icon = this.querySelector('.w-14.h-14');
        if (icon) {
          icon.style.transform = 'scale(1.05)';
          icon.style.transition = 'all 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)';
        }
      });
      
      // Efecto de salida
      card.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
        // Restaurar posición original
        this.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
        this.style.transition = 'all 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)';
        this.style.boxShadow = '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 2px 4px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)';
        
        // Restaurar icono
        const icon = this.querySelector('.w-14.h-14');
        if (icon) {
          icon.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
          icon.style.transition = 'all 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)';
        }
      });
      
      // Efecto de click/tap sutil
      card.addEventListener('mousedown', function() {
        this.style.transform = 'translateY(-2px)';
      });
      
      card.addEventListener('mouseup', function() {
        this.style.transform = 'translateY(-6px)';
      });
    });

    // Selector dinámico de tipo de sitio web
    const websiteSelector = document.getElementById('website-type-selector');
    const priceDisplay = document.getElementById('price-display');
    const selectedPrice = document.getElementById('selected-price');
    const selectedDescription = document.getElementById('selected-description');

    if (websiteSelector && priceDisplay && selectedPrice && selectedDescription) {
      // Detectar idioma desde la URL
      const currentLang = window.location.pathname.startsWith('/en') ? 'en' : 'es';
      const locale = currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'es-CR';
      
      websiteSelector.addEventListener('change', function() {
        const selectedOption = this.options[this.selectedIndex];
        
        if (selectedOption.value) {
          const price = selectedOption.getAttribute('data-price');
          const description = selectedOption.getAttribute('data-desc');
          
          selectedPrice.textContent = `$${Math.round(parseFloat(price)).toLocaleString(locale, { maximumFractionDigits: 0 })}`;
          selectedDescription.textContent = description;
          
          // Mostrar con animación
          priceDisplay.classList.remove('hidden');
          priceDisplay.style.opacity = '0';
          priceDisplay.style.transform = 'translateY(10px)';
          
          setTimeout(() => {
            priceDisplay.style.transition = 'all 0.3s ease-out';
            priceDisplay.style.opacity = '1';
            priceDisplay.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
          }, 50);
        } else {
          // Ocultar con animación
          priceDisplay.style.transition = 'all 0.3s ease-out';
          priceDisplay.style.opacity = '0';
          priceDisplay.style.transform = 'translateY(-10px)';
          
          setTimeout(() => {
            priceDisplay.classList.add('hidden');
          }, 300);
        }
      });
    }
  });
</script>  <section id="portfolio" class="pt-24 pb-20 px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 bg-white relative" data-astro-cid-7kp4msfm> <!-- Grid Background --> <div class="absolute inset-0 opacity-20" formulario </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> </section> <script>(function(){const recaptchaSiteKey = "6LflMTUsAAAAAOH9U6JE-lJMLjxlPjQ4oxgzCRgg";
const errorMessage = "Error al enviar el mensaje. Por favor intenta nuevamente.";
const sending = "Enviando...";
const submitButton = "Enviar mensaje";
const successMessage = "¡Mensaje enviado exitosamente! Te responderemos en menos de 24 horas.";
const apiUrl = "";

  // Hacer disponible la site key de reCAPTCHA globalmente
  if (recaptchaSiteKey) {
    window.RECAPTCHA_SITE_KEY = recaptchaSiteKey;
  }
  
  // Configurar URL del API (para producción con servicio externo)
  if (apiUrl) {
    window.CONTACT_API_URL = apiUrl;
  }
  
  // Datos para el formulario de contacto
  window.contactFormData = {
    loading: false,
    success: false,
    error: '',
    errorMessage: errorMessage,
    sending: sending,
    submitButton: submitButton,
    successMessage: successMessage,
    recaptchaSiteKey: recaptchaSiteKey,
    
    async handleSubmit(event) {
      event.preventDefault();
      this.loading = true;
      this.error = '';
      this.success = false;
      
      const form = event.target;
      const formData = new FormData(form);
      
      // Obtener token de reCAPTCHA si está disponible
      let recaptchaToken = '';
      if (window.grecaptcha && window.grecaptcha.ready && this.recaptchaSiteKey) {
        try {
          await window.grecaptcha.ready(async () => {
            recaptchaToken = await window.grecaptcha.execute(this.recaptchaSiteKey, { action: 'contact_form' });
          });
        } catch (e) {
          console.warn('reCAPTCHA no disponible:', e);
        }
      }
      
      if (recaptchaToken) {
        formData.append('recaptcha_token', recaptchaToken);
      }
      
      try {
        // En producción (SiteGround), usar endpoint PHP
        // En desarrollo, usar endpoint Astro
        const isProduction = window.location.hostname !== 'localhost' && window.location.hostname !== '127.0.0.1';
        const apiUrl = isProduction ? '/api/contact.php' : (window.CONTACT_API_URL || '/api/contact');
        const response = await fetch(apiUrl, {
          method: 'POST',
          body: formData,
        });
        
        const result = await response.json();
        
        if (result.success) {
          this.success = true;
          form.reset();
          // Scroll suave al mensaje de éxito
          setTimeout(() => {
            form.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
          }, 100);
        } else {
          this.error = result.message || result.errors?.rateLimit || result.errors?.recaptcha || result.errors?.honeypot || this.errorMessage;
          // Mostrar errores de campos específicos si existen
          if (result.errors) {
            Object.keys(result.errors).forEach(field => {
              if (field !== 'rateLimit' && field !== 'recaptcha' && field !== 'honeypot') {
                const input = form.querySelector(`[name='${field}']`);
                if (input) {
                  input.classList.add('border-red-500');
                  input.addEventListener('input', () => {
                    input.classList.remove('border-red-500');
                  }, { once: true });
                }
              }
            });
          }
        }
      } catch (err) {
        this.error = this.errorMessage;
        console.error('Error enviando formulario:', err);
      } finally {
        this.loading = false;
      }
    }
  };
})();</script> </main> <footer class="bg-neutral-black text-white"> <div class="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-12"> <!-- Contenido principal del footer --> <div class="grid md:grid-cols-2  <script>
  (function() {
    'use strict';
    
    // Selector y calculadora
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      const modalWebsiteSelector = document.getElementById('modal-website-type-selector');
      const modalPriceDisplay = document.getElementById('modal-price-display');
      const modalSelectedPrice = document.getElementById('modal-selected-price');
      const modalSelectedDescription = document.getElementById('modal-selected-description');
      const extrasCalculator = document.getElementById('extras-calculator');
      const totalPrice = document.getElementById('total-price');

      let basePrice = 0;

      function calculateTotalPrice() {
        let total = basePrice;
        
        const bilingue = document.getElementById('extras-bilingue');
        const crm = document.getElementById('extras-crm');
        const animaciones = document.getElementById('extras-animaciones');
        const blog = document.getElementById('extras-blog');

        if (bilingue && bilingue.checked) total += 113;
        if (crm && crm.checked) total += 95;
        if (animaciones && animaciones.checked) total += 125;
        if (blog && blog.checked) total += 150;

        if (totalPrice) {
          // Detectar idioma desde la URL
          const currentLang = window.location.pathname.startsWith('/en') ? 'en' : 'es';
          const locale = currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'es-CR';
          
          totalPrice.textContent = `$${Math.round(total).toLocaleString(locale, { maximumFractionDigits: 0 })}`;
        }
      }

      if (modalWebsiteSelector && modalPriceDisplay && modalSelectedPrice && modalSelectedDescription) {
        modalWebsiteSelector.addEventListener('change', function() {
          const selectedOption = this.options[this.selectedIndex];
          
          if (selectedOption.value) {
            const price = selectedOption.getAttribute('data-price');
            const description = selectedOption.getAttribute('data-desc');
            
            basePrice = parseFloat(price);
            
            // Detectar idioma desde la URL
            const currentLang = window.location.pathname.startsWith('/en') ? 'en' : 'es';
            const locale = currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'es-CR';
            
            modalSelectedPrice.textContent = `$${Math.round(basePrice).toLocaleString(locale, { maximumFractionDigits: 0 })}`;
            modalSelectedDescription.textContent = description;
            
            // Mostrar
            modalPriceDisplay.classList.remove('hidden');
            modalPriceDisplay.style.opacity = '0';
            modalPriceDisplay.style.transform = 'translateY(10px)';
            
            setTimeout(() => {
              modalPriceDisplay.style.transition = 'all 0.3s ease-out';
              modalPriceDisplay.style.opacity = '1';
              modalPriceDisplay.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
            }, 50);

            // Mostrar calculadora
            if (extrasCalculator) {
              extrasCalculator.style.display = 'block';
              extrasCalculator.style.opacity = '0';
              extrasCalculator.style.transform = 'translateY(20px)';
              
              setTimeout(() => {
                extrasCalculator.style.transition = 'all 0.3s ease-out';
                extrasCalculator.style.opacity = '1';
                extrasCalculator.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
              }, 200);
            }

            calculateTotalPrice();
          } else {
            // Ocultar
            modalPriceDisplay.style.transition = 'all 0.3s ease-out';
            modalPriceDisplay.style.opacity = '0';
            modalPriceDisplay.style.transform = 'translateY(-10px)';
            
            setTimeout(() => {
              modalPriceDisplay.classList.add('hidden');
            }, 300);

            if (extrasCalculator) {
              extrasCalculator.style.transition = 'all 0.3s ease-out';
              extrasCalculator.style.opacity = '0';
              extrasCalculator.style.transform = 'translateY(-20px)';
              
              setTimeout(() => {
                extrasCalculator.style.display = 'none';
              }, 300);
            }
          }
        });
      }

      // Event listeners para extras
      const extraCheckboxes = ['extras-bilingue', 'extras-crm', 'extras-animaciones', 'extras-blog'];
      extraCheckboxes.forEach(id => {
        const checkbox = document.getElementById(id);
        if (checkbox) {
          checkbox.addEventListener('change', calculateTotalPrice);
        }
      });
    });
  })();
</script> <div id="hosting-modal" class="fixed inset-0 z-50 hidden overflow-hidden" aria-labelledby="hosting-modal-title" aria-modal="true" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <!-- Overlay transparente --> <div class="absolute inset-0 bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm transition-opacity" onclick="closeModal('hosting-modal')" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx></div> <!-- Modal Container --> <div class="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center p-4 pointer-events-none" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <div class="modal-container relative w-full max-w-6xl rounded-2xl bg-white shadow-2xl transform transition-all pointer-events-auto" onclick="event.stopPropagation()" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <!-- Header - Fixed (Sin gradiente, diseño limpio) --> <div class="flex-shrink-0 bg-white border-b border-gray-200 px-6 py-5 md:py-5 py-3 rounded-t-2xl" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <div class="flex items-center justify-between" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <h3 id="hosting-modal-title" class="text-2xl md:text-2xl text-xl font-bold" style="color: var(--sd-gray-dark-5);" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> Hosting Premium y Correos </h3> <button onclick="closeModal('hosting-modal')" class="rounded-lg bg-gray-100 hover:bg-gray-200 p-2.5 md:p-2.5 p-2 transition-all duration-200 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2" style="color: var(--sd-gray-dark-5); <script>
  (function() {
    'use strict';
    // Calculadora de Google Workspace
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      const workspaceUsers = document.getElementById('workspace-users');
      const workspaceTotal = document.getElementById('workspace-total');

      if (workspaceUsers && workspaceTotal) {
        function calculateWorkspaceTotal() {
          const users = parseInt(workspaceUsers.value) || 1;
          const pricePerUser = 32.50;
          const total = users * pricePerUser;
          
          // Detectar idioma desde la URL
          const currentLang = window.location.pathname.startsWith('/en') ? 'en' : 'es';
          const locale = currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'es-CR';
          
          workspaceTotal.textContent = `$${Math.round(total).toLocaleString(locale, { maximumFractionDigits: 0 })}`;
        }

        workspaceUsers.addEventListener('input', calculateWorkspaceTotal);
        calculateWorkspaceTotal();
      }
    });
  })();
</script> <div id="maintenance-modal" class="fixed inset-0 z-50 hidden overflow-hidden" aria-labelledby="maintenance-modal-title" aria-modal="true" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <!-- Overlay transparente --> <div class="absolute inset-0 bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm transition-opacity" onclick="closeModal('maintenance-modal')" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx></div> <!-- Modal Container --> <div class="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center p-4 pointer-events-none" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <div class="modal-container relative w-full max-w-6xl rounded-2xl bg-white shadow-2xl transform transition-all pointer-events-auto" onclick="event.stopPropagation()" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <!-- Header - Fixed (Sin gradiente, diseño limpio) --> <div class="flex-shrink-0 bg-white border-b border-gray-200 px-6 py-5 md:py-5 py-3 rounded-t-2xl" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <div class="flex items-center justify-between" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <h3 id="maintenance-modal-title" class="text-2xl md:text-2xl text-xl font-bold" style="color: var(--sd-gray-dark-5);" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> Mantenimiento Web </h3> <button onclick="closeModal('maintenance-modal')" class="rounded-lg bg-gray-100 hover:bg-gray-200 p-2.5 md:p-2.5 p-2 transition-all duration-200 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2" style="color: var(--sd-gray-dark-5);   (function() {
    'use strict';
    // Calculadora
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      const disenoTotal = document.getElementById('diseno-total');
      const checkboxes = [
        { id: 'calc-arte-publicitario', price: 77 },
        { id: 'calc-animacion-logo', price: 160 },
        { id: 'calc-cortinillas', price: 95 },
        { id: 'calc-interfaces', price: 533 }
      ];

      function calculateDisenoTotal() {
        let total = 0;
        checkboxes.forEach(item => {
          const checkbox = document.getElementById(item.id);
          if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
            total += item.price;
          }
        });
        if (disenoTotal) {
          disenoTotal.textContent = `$${Math.round(total).toLocaleString('es-CR', { maximumFractionDigits: 0 })}`;
        }
      }

      checkboxes.forEach(item => {
        const checkbox = document.getElementById(item.id);
        if (checkbox) {
          checkbox.addEventListener('change', calculateDisenoTotal);
        }
      });

      calculateDisenoTotal();
    });
  })();

Solicitar Información
</a> </div>  </div> <!-- Footer - Fixed (Simplificado) --> <div class="flex-shrink-0 bg-white px-6 py-4 md:py-4 py-3 border-t border-gray-200 flex justify-center rounded-b-2xl" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> <a href="#contact" onclick="closeModal('marketing-modal')" class="inline-flex justify-center rounded-lg px-8 py-3 md:px-8 md:py-3 px-6 py-2.5 text-base md:text-base text-sm font-bold text-white shadow-lg hover:shadow-xl focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2 transition-all duration-200 transform hover:scale-105" style="background-color: var(--sd-green-300); color: var(--sd-gray-dark-5);" data-astro-cid-hiqpehsx> Solicitar Información </a> </div> </div> </div> </div>   <script>
  (function() {
    'use strict';
    // Calculadora de ROI
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      const roiBudget = document.getElementById('roi-budget');
      const roiConversion = document.getElementById('roi-conversion');
      const roiValue = document.getElementById('roi-value');
      const roiResult = document.getElementById('roi-result');
      const roiClients = document.getElementById('roi-clients');
      const roiRevenue = document.getElementById('roi-revenue');

      function calculateROI() {
        const budget = parseFloat(roiBudget.value) || 1000;
        const conversion = parseFloat(roiConversion.value) || 3;
        const value = parseFloat(roiValue.value) || 200;
        
        const clicks = budget * 0.1;
        const clients = Math.round(clicks * (conversion / 100));
        const revenue = clients * value;
        const roi = Math.round(((revenue - budget) / budget) * 100);

        if (roiResult) roiResult.textContent = `${roi}%`;
        if (roiClients) roiClients.textContent = clients;
        if (roiRevenue) roiRevenue.textContent = revenue.toLocaleString('es-CR');
      }

      if (roiBudget) roiBudget.addEventListener('input', calculateROI);
      if (roiConversion) roiConversion.addEventListener('input', calculateROI);
      if (roiValue) roiValue.addEventListener('input', calculateROI);

      calculateROI();
    });
  })();

  (function() {
    'use strict';
    // Calculadora
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      const consultoriaSessions = document.getElementById('consultoria-sessions');
      const consultoriaTotal = document.getElementById('consultoria-total');

      if (consultoriaSessions && consultoriaTotal) {
        function calculateConsultoriaTotal() {
          const sessions = parseInt(consultoriaSessions.value) || 1;
          const pricePerSession = 200.00;
          const total = sessions * pricePerSession;
          
          consultoriaTotal.textContent = `$${Math.round(total).toLocaleString('es-CR', { maximumFractionDigits: 0 })}`;
        }

        consultoriaSessions.addEventListener('input', calculateConsultoriaTotal);
        calculateConsultoriaTotal();
      }
    });
  })();
</script>  </div> <!-- Cookie Consent System --> ---
